# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
- Can be added ^qyog6UiQ

What do we know about vectors? ^ZI3DVaeE

- Direction AND magnitude ^YlNk7jqa

- In the format: ^l9NLqEgR

- -ve is same length opposite direction ^YamVVEF9

i is a unit vector in the x direction
j is a unit vector in the y direction

k is a unit vector in the z direction ^Xxvo6ldW

2 vectors are parallel if one is a multiple of the other
2 vectors are co-linear if they are parallel and share a point ^HNUrZ3d6

If a is a vector,  then the unit vector a in the same direction is: ^W6DTh4St
